***buks.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buks.html>buks</a> (61521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Büchse</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullebak.html>bullebak</a> (17233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bul.html>bul</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bak.html>bak</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullock.html>bullock</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular <a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bullocks.html>bullocks</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bullocking</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bullocked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>To</a> bully.

<p>Either <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bult.html>bult</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hump.html>hump</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:back.html>back</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> shortening <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bultrugwalvis</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bunker.html>bunker</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***burcht.html

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>With</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:seemingly.html>seemingly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:random.html>random</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:addition.html>addition</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i>-t</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">burch</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*burg</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*burg</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*burgz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰerǵʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortified elevation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
